This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. We only want to change\\n274:     # the default when neither have been user-specified. Note that we default to foreach\\n275:     # and pass False to use_fused. This is not a mistake--we want to give the fused impl\\n276:     # bake-in time before making it the default, even if it is typically faster.\\n277:     if foreach is None and fused is None:\\n278:         # why must we be explicit about an if statement for torch.jit.is_scripting here?\\n279:         # because JIT can't handle Optionals nor fancy conditionals when scripting\\n280:         if not torch.jit.is_scripting():\\n295:         raise RuntimeError(\\\"torch.jit.script not supported with fused optimizers\\\")\\n296: \\n297:     if foreach and not torch.jit.is_scripting():\\n298:         func = _multi_tensor_sgd\\n299:     elif fused and not torch.jit.is_scripting():\\n300:         func = _fused_sgd\\n301:     else:\\n302:         func = _single_tensor_sgd\\n303: \\n304:     func(\\n305:         params,\\n306:         d_p_list,\\n307:         momentum_buffer_list,\\n308:         weight_decay=weight_decay,\\n309:         momentum=momentum,\\n310:         lr=lr,\\n311:         dampening=dampening,\\n312:         nesterov=nesterov,\\n313:         has_sparse_grad=has_sparse_grad,\\n314:         maximize=maximize,\\n315:         grad_scale=grad_scale,\\n316:         found_inf=found_inf,\\n317:     )\\n318: \\n319: \\n320: def _single_tensor_sgd(\\n321:     params: list[Tensor],\\n322:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n323:     momentum_buffer_list: \\n337:     if not torch.jit.is_scripting():\\n338:         lr = _to_scalar(lr)\\n339: \\n340:     for i, param in enumerate(params):\\n341:         grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\\n342: \\n343:         if weight_decay != 0:\\n344:             # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\\n345:             if isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\\n346: This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. \n186:     Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n187:     `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n188:     \"\"\"\n189:     + rf\"\"\"\n190:     Args:\n191: This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n245: \n246:     \"\"\"\n247: )\n248: \n249: \n250: def sgd(\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n261:     *,\n262:     weight_decay: float,\n263:     momentum: float,\n264:     lr: float,\n265:     dampening: float,\n266:     nesterov: bool,\n267:     maximize: bool,\n268: ):\n269:     r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n270: \n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n272:     \"\"\"\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. We only want to change\n    # the default when neither have been user-specified. Note that we default to foreach\n    # and pass False to use_fused. This is not a mistake--we want to give the fused impl\n    # bake-in time before making it the default, even if it is typically faster.\n    if foreach is None and fused is None:\n        # why must we be explicit about an if statement for torch.jit.is_scripting here?\n        # because JIT can't handle Optionals nor fancy conditionals when scripting\n        if not torch.jit.is_scripting():\n            fused, foreach = _default_to_fused_or_foreach(\n                params, differentiable=False, use_fused=False\n            )\n        else:\n            foreach = False\n            fused = False\n    if foreach is None:\n        foreach = False\n    if fused is None:\n        fused = False\n\n    if foreach and torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        raise RuntimeError(\"torch.jit.script not supported with foreach optimizers\")\n    if fused and torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        raise RuntimeError(\"torch.jit.script not supported with fused optimizers\")\n\n    if foreach and not torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        func = _multi_tensor_sgd\n    elif fused and not torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        func = _fused_sgd\n    else:\n        func = _single_tensor_sgd\n\n    func(\n        params,\n        d_p_list,\n        momentum_buffer_list,\n        weight_decay=weight_decay,\n        momentum=momentum,\n        lr=lr,\n        dampening=dampening,\n        nesterov=nesterov,\n        has_sparse_grad=has_sparse_grad,\n        maximize=maximize,\n        grad_scale=grad_scale,\n        found_inf=found_inf,\n    )\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n    has_sparse_grad: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if not torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                    # usually this is the differentiable path, which is why the param.clone() is needed\n                    grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n            else:\n                grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if momentum != 0:\n            buf = momentum_buffer_list[i]\n\n            if buf is None:\n                buf = grad.detach().clone()\n                momentum_buffer_list[i] = buf\n            else:\n                buf.mul_(momentum).add_(grad, alpha=1 - dampening)\n\n            if nesterov:\n                grad = grad.add(buf, alpha=momentum)\n            else:\n                grad = buf\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n            if lr.requires_grad:\n                param.addcmul_(grad, lr, value=-1)\n            else:\n                param.add_(grad, alpha=-lr)\n        else:\n            param.add_(grad, alpha=-lr)\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n    has_sparse_grad: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, momentum_buffer_list],  # type: ignore[list-item]\n        with_indices=True,\n    )\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_momentum_buffer_list,\n    ), indices in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n\n        device_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(\n            grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads\n        )\n\n        # Use shared utilities from _foreach module\n        if maximize:\n            device_grads = _foreach_neg_if_maximize(device_grads, True)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n            device_grads = _foreach_add_weight_decay(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize\n            )\n\n        if momentum != 0:\n            bufs: list[Tensor] = []\n\n            all_states_with_momentum_buffer = True\n            for i in range(len(device_momentum_buffer_list)):\n                if device_momentum_buffer_list[i] is None:\n                    all_states_with_momentum_buffer = False\n                    break\n                else:\n                    bufs.append(cast(Tensor, device_momentum_buffer_list[i]))\n\n            if all_states_with_momentum_buffer:\n                torch._foreach_mul_(bufs, momentum)\n                torch._foreach_add_(bufs, device_grads, alpha=1 - dampening)\n            else:\n                bufs = []\n                for i in range(len(device_momentum_buffer_list)):\n                    if device_momentum_buffer_list[i] is None:\n                        buf = device_momentum_buffer_list[i] = momentum_buffer_list[\n                            indices[i]\n                        ] = device_grads[i].detach().clone()\n                    else:\n                        buf = cast(Tensor, device_momentum_buffer_list[i])\n                        buf.mul_(momentum).add_(device_grads[i], alpha=1 - dampening)\n\n                    bufs.append(buf)\n\n            if nesterov:\n                torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, bufs, alpha=momentum)\n            else:\n                device_grads = bufs\n\n        if not device_has_sparse_grad:\n            # foreach APIs don't support sparse\n            for i in range(len(device_params)):\n                device_params[i].add_(device_grads[i], alpha=-lr)\n\n\ndef _fused_sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n    has_sparse_grad: bool,\n) -> None:\n    if not params:\n        return\n    if has_sparse_grad:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"`_fused_sgd` does not support sparse gradients\")\n    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n    )\n    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n    )\n\n    no_momentum_buffer = momentum == 0\n    is_first_step = (\n        all(t is None for t in momentum_buffer_list) and not no_momentum_buffer\n    )\n    if is_first_step:\n        for i, g in enumerate(grads):\n            momentum_buffer_list[i] = torch.empty_like(g)\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, momentum_buffer_list],  # type: ignore[list-item]\n        with_indices=False,\n    )\n    for (device, _), (\n        (device_params_, device_grads_, device_momentum_buffer_list),\n        _,\n    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n        device_params: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n        if grad_scale is not None:\n            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n                device, grad_scale.to(device)\n            )\n        if found_inf_dict is not None and found_inf is not None:\n            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(device, found_inf.to(device))\n        torch._fused_sgd_(\n            device_params,\n            device_grads,\n            []\n            if no_momentum_buffer\n            else cast(list[Tensor], device_momentum_buffer_list),\n            weight_decay=weight_decay,\n            momentum=momentum,\n            lr=lr,\n            dampening=dampening,\n            nesterov=nesterov,\n            maximize=maximize,\n            is_first_step=is_first_step,\n            grad_scale=device_grad_scale,\n            found_inf=device_found_inf,\n        )\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

\\\\textit{amsgrad},\\n283:                 \\\\:\\\\textit{maximize},  \\\\: \\\\epsilon \\\\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\\\\\\n284:             &\\\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:                   \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:    \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow \\\\big(\\\\sqrt{\\\\widehat{v_t}} + \\\\epsilon \\\\big)                                       \\\\\\\\\\n305:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\\n326:         amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\\n327:             algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\\n328:             (default: False)\\n329:         {_foreach_doc}\\n330:         {_maximize_doc}\\n331:         {_capturable_doc}\\n332:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n333:         {_fused_doc}\\n334:     .. \\n345: def _single_tensor_adam(\\n346:     params: list[Tensor],\\n347:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n348:     exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\\n349:     exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\\n350:     max_exp_avg_sqs: \\n273: \\n274: Adam.__doc__ = (\\n275:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Implements Adam algorithm.\\n276: \\n277:     .. math::\\n278:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n279:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n280:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\beta_1, \\\\beta_2\\n281:                 \\\\text{ (betas)},\\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)},f(\\\\theta) \\\\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\\\\\\n282:             &\\\\hspace{13mm}      \\\\lambda \\\\text{ (weight decay)},  \\\\: &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n291:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n295:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\\\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\\\\\\n296:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance.   .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # amsgrad,\n            \"maximize\": maximize,\n            \"foreach\": foreach,\n            \"capturable\": capturable,\n            \"differentiable\": differentiable,\n            \"fused\": fused,\n            \"decoupled_weight_decay\": decoupled_weight_decay,\n        }\n        super().__init__(params, defaults)\n\n        if fused:\n            if differentiable:\n                raise RuntimeError(\"`fused` does not support `differentiable`\")\n            self._step_supports_amp_scaling = True\n            # TODO(crcrpar): [low prec params & their higher prec copy]\n            # Support AMP with FP16/BF16 model params which would need\n            # higher prec copy of params to do update math in higher prec to\n            # alleviate the loss of information.\n self.param_groups:\n            group.setdefault(\"amsgrad\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"maximize\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"foreach\", None)\n            group.setdefault(\"capturable\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"differentiable\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"decoupled_weight_decay\", False)\n            fused = group.setdefault(\"fused\", None)\n            for p in group[\"params\"]:\n                p_state = self.state.get(p, [])\n                if len(p_state) != 0 and not torch.is_tensor(p_state[\"step\"]):\n                    step_val = float(p_state[\"step\"])\n                    p_state[\"step\"] = (\n                        torch.tensor(\n                            step_val,\n                            dtype=_get_scalar_dtype(is_fused=fused),\n                            device=p.device,\n                        )\n                        if group,\n        params_with_grad,\n        grads,\n        exp_avgs,\n        exp_avg_sqs,\n        max_exp_avg_sqs,\n        state_steps,\n    ):\n        has_complex = False\n        for p in group[\"params\"]:\n            if p.grad is not None:\n                has_complex |= torch.is_complex(p)\n                params_with_grad.append(p)\n                if p.grad.is_sparse:\n                    raise RuntimeError(\n                        \"Adam does not support sparse gradients, please consider SparseAdam instead\"\n                    )\n                grads.append(p.grad)\n\n                state = self.state[p]\n                # Lazy state initialization\n                if len(state) == 0:\n                    if group[\"fused\"]:\n                        _device_dtype_check_for_fused(p)\n                    # note(crcrpar): [special device hosting for step]\n                    # Deliberately host `step` on CPU if both capturable and fused are off.\n                    # This is because kernel launches are costly on CUDA and XLA.\n                    state[\"step\"] = (\n                        torch.zeros(\n                            (),\n                            dtype=_get_scalar_dtype(is_fused=group[\"fused\"]),\n                            device=p.device,\n                        )\n                        if group[\"capturable\"] or group[\"fused\"]\n                        else torch.tensor(0.0, dtype=_get_scalar_dtype())\n                    )\n                    # Exponential moving average of gradient values\n                    state[\"exp_avg\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                    )\n                    # Exponential moving average of squared gradient values\n                    state[\"exp_avg_sq\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                    )\n                    if group[\"amsgrad\"]:\n                        # Maintains max of all exp. moving avg. of sq. grad. values\n                        state[\"max_exp_avg_sq\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n                            p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                        )\n\n                exp_avgs.append(state[\"exp_avg\"])\n                exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"exp_avg_sq\"])\n\n                if group[\"amsgrad\"]:\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"max_exp_avg_sq\"])\n                if group[\"differentiable\"] and state[\"step\"].requires_grad:\n                    raise RuntimeError(\n                        \"`requires_grad` is not supported for `step` in differentiable mode\"\n                    )\n\n                # Foreach without capturable does not support a tensor lr\n                if (\n                    group[\"foreach\"]\n                    and torch.is_tensor(group[\"lr\"])\n                    and not group[\"capturable\"]\n                ):\n                    raise RuntimeError(\n                        \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n                    )\n\n                state_steps.append(state[\"step\"])\n        return has_complex\n\n    @_use_grad_for_differentiable\n    def step(self, closure=None):\n        \"\"\"Perform a single optimization step.\n\n        Args:\n            closure (Callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model\n                and returns the loss.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._cuda_graph_capture_health_check()\n\n        loss = None\n        if closure is not None:\n            with torch.enable_grad():\n                loss = closure()\n\n        for group in self.param_groups:\n            params_with_grad: list[Tensor] = []\n            grads: list[Tensor] = []\n            exp_avgs: list[Tensor] = []\n            exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n            max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n grads,\n                exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sqs,\n                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                state_steps,\n            )\n\n            adam(\n                params_with_grad,\n   .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n\n        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n\n        # Handle complex parameters\n        if has_complex:\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params,\n                    device_grads,\n                    device_exp_avgs,\n                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                )\n            else:\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n                )\n\n        # Use shared utility from _foreach module\n        if maximize:\n            device_grads = _foreach_neg_if_maximize(device_grads, True)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        # Update steps\n        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                device_grads = _foreach_add_weight_decay(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                    device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize\n                )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n        # tensors are on the same device\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n        )\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n\n        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1.0\n        else:\n            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1 - beta2\n\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del device_grads\n        del scaled_device_grads\n\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  #
